Vintage Super League Season 7 Decklists
=======================================



 Posted in **Magic Online**
 on December 6, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast











Below are the decklists for the Vintage Super League's seventh season.


Vintage Super League (VSL) is a series of competitive *Magic Online* matches between *Magic*'s most well-known players taken place on our [Twitch](https://www.twitch.tv/magic) channel every Tuesday night at 5 p.m. Pacific Time. Did you miss a stream? No worries! Head over to our [YouTube](https://www.youtube.com/user/wizardsmtg) channel to catch up on past events.


Follow the links below to take you to the corresponding decklist.


* [VSL Season 7 Finals Decklists](#FINALS)
	+ [Kevin Cron: 1BR, Thoughtcast Outcome, Ballista Shops](#Kevin%20Cron%20FINALS)
	+ [Reid Duke: Bargain Storm, Bob's Revenge, Mishra's Workshop](#Reid%20Duke%20FINALS)
* [Grudge Match Decklists](#Grudge%20Match)
	+ [Stephen Menendian: Burning Oath, Woke Mentor, PO Mentor](#Stephen%20Grudge%20Match)
	+ [Rich Shay: Leyline Dredge, Sylvan Walkers, Foundry Shops](#Stephen%20Grudge%20Match)
* [Playoffs Week 1 Decklists](#Playoff%20Week%201)
	+ [Bob Maher: Otah, Ravager Shops, and Outcome](#Bob%20Maher%20Playoff%20W1)
	+ [Kevin Cron: Shops, 1BR, and Jeskai Outcome](#Kevin%20Cron%20Playoffs%20W1)
	+ [Eric Froehlich: Workshops, Pyro, and Outcome](#Eric%20Froehlich%20Playoffs%20W1)
* [Week 9 Decklists](#Week9)
